 yah seva shuru karne vaala yah desh kaa pehla stesan he

 Addressing senior railway officials, Google personnel and passengers at the suburb railway station, Prabhu said, 'when i proposed the full (rail) budget last year, i resolved to rectify the bad condition of Indian Railways and Mumbai Central The introduction of free wi-fi at the station is a major step towards the improvement of the railway
 ’ Describing the facility as 'world class', Prabhu said that around 100 busy stations in the country will be brought under free public wi-fi service by the end of this year and this is the world's largest project

 Khudiram Bose started taking part in political activities from the days of school against those of English imperialism
